Management Architecture\\n\\nThe consumer offset management in Apache Kafka is implemented across the following key components:\\n\\n### Core Data Structures\\n\\n1. **OffsetAndMetadata** - Represents a committed offset with metadata:\\n   - Server-side implementation: `group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetAndMetadata.java` - Stores offset, leader epoch, metadata, commit timestamp, and topic ID\\n   - Client-side implementation: `clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/OffsetAndMetadata.java` - Used by consumers to track offsets\\n\\n### Storage in __consumer_offsets Topic\\n\\nOffsets are persisted as records in the `__consumer_offsets` internal topic with:\\n- **OffsetCommitKey** and **OffsetCommitValue** generated records (from protocol definition)\\n- Records contain group ID, topic, partition, offset, metadata, and timestamps\\n- **Log compaction** maintains only the latest offset for each group-topic-partition combination\\n\\n### GroupCoordinator Interface and Implementation\\n\\nThe offset commit/fetch handler is the `GroupCoordinator` interface (`group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinator.java`) with implementations:\\n\\n- **GroupCoordinatorService** (`group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorService.java`) - High-level coordinator service that delegates to shard\\n- **GroupCoordinatorShard** (`group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorShard.java`) - Replicated state machine handling offset commit/fetch for a specific partition\\n\\n#### Offset Commit Handler\\nThe commit flow:\\n1. **handleOffsetCommitRequest** in `KafkaApis.scala` - Receives OffsetCommitRequest from client\\n2. Routes to **GroupCoordinator.handleOffsetCommit** via GroupCoordinatorService\\n3. **GroupCoordinatorShard.handleOffsetCommit** - Processes and generates CoordinatorRecords\\n4. **OffsetMetadataManager.handleCommitOffsets** - Stores offset in memory and generates write records\\n\\n#### OffsetFetch Request Processor\\nThe fetch flow:\\n1. **handleOffsetFetchRequest** in `KafkaApis.scala` - Receives OffsetFetchRequest\\n2. Routes to **GroupCoordinator.fetchOffsets** via GroupCoordinatorService\\n3. **GroupCoordinatorShard.handleOffsetFetch** - Validates authorization\\n4. **OffsetMetadataManager.fetchOffsets** - Retrieves offsets from memory\\n\\n### OffsetMetadataManager - Core Offset Storage\\n\\nThe `OffsetMetadataManager` (`group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetMetadataManager.java`) manages:\\n- **offsets** - Timeline HashMap storing group -> topic -> partition -> OffsetAndMetadata\\n- **pendingTransactionalOffsets** - Tracks transactional offsets not yet committed\\n- **openTransactions** - Tracks groups with ongoing transactions\\n\\nKey methods:\\n- **handleCommitOffsets** - Handles offset commit requests and generates tombstone records for replacements\\n- **fetchOffsets** - Retrieves committed offsets for fetch requests\\n- **deleteOffsets** - Deletes offsets (OffsetDelete API)\\n- **onPartitionsDeleted** - Cleans up offsets when topics are deleted\\n- **cleanupExpiredOffsets** - Removes expired offsets\\n\\n### Offset Expiry and Compaction Logic\\n\\n**OffsetExpirationCondition** interface (`group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetExpirationCondition.java`) defines when an offset expires:\\n\\n**OffsetExpirationConditionImpl** (`group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetExpirationConditionImpl.java`) implements expiration based on:\\n- Base timestamp (commit timestamp for consumer offsets)\\n- Configured retention period (offsets.retention.minutes)\\n- Current time\\n\\n**Offset cleanup** in `OffsetMetadataManager.cleanupExpiredOffsets`:\\n- Iterates through all offsets for groups not subscribed to topics\\n- Checks if offset has expired using OffsetExpirationCondition\\n- Appends tombstone records (null values) for expired offsets\\n- Tombstone records enable log compaction to remove old entries\\n- Records cleanup metric via OFFSET_EXPIRED_SENSOR_NAME\\n\\n**Log Compaction**: The __consumer_offsets topic uses log compaction (cleanup.policy=compact):\\n- Tombstone records (null values) mark deleted offsets\\n- Log cleaner removes entries with identical keys and null values\\n- Maintains only the latest offset for each group-topic-partition\\n\\n### Group Metadata Management\\n\\nThe `GroupMetadataManager` (`group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupMetadataManager.java`) tracks:\\n- Group lifecycle and state\\n- Which groups have active offsets\\n- Group expiration conditions\\n\\nDifferent group types support different offset expiration:\\n- **ClassicGroup** - Expires based on last commit timestamp\\n- **ConsumerGroup** - Expires based on last commit timestamp  \\n- **StreamsGroup** - Expires based on last commit timestamp\\n- **ShareGroup** - Does not support offset expiration\\n\\n### Request/Response Protocol\\n\\nThe offset management uses these protocol requests/responses:\\n- **OffsetCommitRequest/Response** - Commits offsets for a consumer group\\n- **OffsetFetchRequest/Response** - Fetches committed offsets\\n- **OffsetDeleteRequest/Response** - Deletes offsets (Admin API)\\n\\nProtocol definitions automatically generate key/value classes for __consumer_offsets records.\\n\\n### Configuration\\n\\n`GroupCoordinatorConfig` defines critical offset settings:\\n- offsetsRetentionMs - records (from protocol definition)\\n- Records contain group ID, topic, partition, offset, metadata, and timestamps\\n- **Log compaction** maintains only the latest offset for each group-topic-partition combination\\n\\n### GroupCoordinator Interface and Implementation\\n\\nThe offset commit/fetch handler is the `GroupCoordinator` interface Commit Handler\\nThe commit flow:\\n1. **handleOffsetCommitRequest** in `KafkaApis.scala` - Receives OffsetCommitRequest from client\\n2.
